[[H6258|But now]] [[H4994|please]] [[H8085|listen,]] [[H113|O my lord]] [[H4428|the king.]] [[H8467|May my petition]] [[H5307|come]] [[H6440|before you.]] [[H408|Do not]] [[H7725|send me back]] [[H1004|to the house]] [[H3083|of Jonathan]] [[H5608|the scribe,]] [[H3808|or]] [[H4191|I will die]] [[H8033|there.”]] ^3720

[[H4428|So King]] [[H6667|Zedekiah]] [[H6680|gave orders,]] [[H3414|and Jeremiah]] [[H6485|was placed]] [[H2691|in the courtyard]] [[H4307|of the guard]] [[H5414|and given]] [[H3603|a loaf]] [[H3899|of bread]] [[H3117|daily]] [[H4480|from]] [[H644|the baker’s]] [[H2351|street,]] [[H5704|until]] [[H3605|all]] [[H3899|the bread]] [[H5892|in the city]] [[H8552|was gone.]] [[H3414|So Jeremiah]] [[H3427|remained]] [[H2691|in the courtyard]] [[H4307|of the guard.]] ^3721

[[H8203|Now Shephatiah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H4977|of Mattan,]] [[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H6583|of Pashhur,]] [[H3116|Jucal]] [[H1121|son]] [[H8018|of Shelemiah,]] [[H6583|and Pashhur]] [[H1121|son]] [[H4441|of Malchijah]] [[H8085|heard]] [[H1697|the words]] [[H3414|Jeremiah]] [[H1696|was telling]] [[H3605|all]] [[H5971|the people:]] ^3801

[[H3541|“This is what]] [[H3068|the LORD]] [[H559|says:]] [[H3427|Whoever stays]] [[H2063|in this]] [[H5892|city]] [[H4191|will die]] [[H2719|by sword,]] [[H7458|famine,]] [[H1698|and plague,]] [[H3318|but whoever surrenders]] [[H413|to]] [[H3778|the Chaldeans]] [[H2421|will live.]] [[H1961|He will escape]] [[H5315|with his life]] [[H7998|as a reward]] [[H2421|and will live.]] ^3802

[[H3541|This is what]] [[H3068|the LORD]] [[H559|says:]] [[H2063|This]] [[H5892|city]] [[H5414|will surely be handed over]] [[H2428|to the army]] [[H4428|of the king]] [[H894|of Babylon,]] [[H3920|and he will capture it.”]] ^3803

[[H8269|Then the officials]] [[H559|said]] [[H413|to]] [[H4428|the king,]] [[H2088|“This]] [[H376|man]] [[H4191|ought to die,]] [[H3588|for]] [[H1931|he]] [[H7503|is discouraging]] [[H376|the warriors]] [[H7604|who remain]] [[H2063|in this]] [[H5892|city,]] [[H3605|as well as all]] [[H5971|the people,]] [[H1696|by speaking]] [[H428|such]] [[H1697|words]] [[H413|to them;]] [[H2088|this]] [[H376|man]] [[H369|is not]] [[H1875|seeking]] [[H7965|the well-being]] [[H2088|of these]] [[H5971|people,]] [[H3588|but]] [[H7451|their ruin.]] ^3804

[[H2009|“Here]] [[H1931|he is,”]] [[H559|replied]] [[H4428|King]] [[H6667|Zedekiah.]] [[H3027|“He is in your hands,]] [[H3588|since]] [[H4428|the king]] [[H369|can do nothing]] [[H1697|to stop you.”]] ^3805

[[H3947|So they took]] [[H3414|Jeremiah]] [[H7993|and dropped]] [[H413|him into]] [[H953|the cistern]] [[H4441|of Malchiah,]] [[H4429|the king’s]] [[H1121|son,]] [[H834|which]] [[H2691|was in the courtyard]] [[H4307|of the guard.]] [[H7971|They lowered]] [[H3414|Jeremiah]] [[H2256|with ropes]] [[H953|into the cistern,]] [[H369|which had no]] [[H4325|water]] [[H3588|but only]] [[H2916|mud,]] [[H3414|and Jeremiah]] [[H2883|sank down]] [[H2916|into the mud.]] ^3806

[[H5663|Now Ebed-melech]] [[H3569|the Cushite,]] [[H5631|a court official]] [[H4428|in the royal]] [[H1004|palace,]] [[H8085|heard]] [[H3414|that Jeremiah]] [[H5414|had been put]] [[H413|into]] [[H953|the cistern.]] [[H4428|While the king]] [[H3427|was sitting]] [[H8179|at the Gate]] [[H1144|of Benjamin,]] ^3807

[[H5663|Ebed-melech]] [[H3318|went out]] [[H4428|from the king’s]] [[H1004|palace]] [[H1696|and said]] [[H413|to]] [[H4428|the king,]] ^3808

[[H113|“My lord]] [[H4428|the king,]] [[H428|these]] [[H376|men]] [[H7489|have acted wickedly]] [[H3605|in all that]] [[H6213|they have done]] [[H3414|to Jeremiah]] [[H5030|the prophet.]] [[H7993|They have dropped]] [[H834|him]] [[H413|into]] [[H953|the cistern,]] [[H8478|where]] [[H4191|he will starve to death,]] [[H3588|for]] [[H369|there is no]] [[H5750|more]] [[H3899|bread]] [[H5892|in the city.”]] ^3809

[[H4428|So the king]] [[H6680|commanded]] [[H5663|Ebed-melech]] [[H3569|the Cushite,]] [[H3947|“Take]] [[H7970|thirty]] [[H376|men]] [[H4480|from]] [[H2088|here]] [[H3027|with you]] [[H5927|and pull]] [[H3414|Jeremiah]] [[H5030|the prophet]] [[H953|out of the cistern]] [[H2962|before]] [[H4191|he dies.”]] ^3810

[[H5663|Then Ebed-melech]] [[H3947|took]] [[H376|the men]] [[H3027|with him]] [[H935|and went]] [[H4428|to the king’s]] [[H1004|palace,]] [[H413|to]] [[H8478|a place below]] [[H214|the storehouse.]] [[H8033|From there]] [[H3947|he took]] [[H1094|old]] [[H5499|rags]] [[H1094|and worn-out]] [[H4418|clothes]] [[H7971|and lowered them]] [[H2256|with ropes]] [[H413|to]] [[H3414|Jeremiah]] [[H413|in]] [[H953|the cistern.]] ^3811

[[H3414|and they pulled him]] [[H4900|up]] [[H2256|with the ropes]] [[H5927|and lifted]] [[H853|him]] [[H4480|out of]] [[H953|the cistern.]] [[H3414|And Jeremiah]] [[H3427|remained]] [[H2691|in the courtyard]] [[H4307|of the guard.]] ^3813

[[H4428|Then King]] [[H6667|Zedekiah]] [[H7971|sent for]] [[H3414|Jeremiah]] [[H5030|the prophet]] [[H3947|and received]] [[H853|him]] [[H413|at]] [[H7992|the third]] [[H3996|entrance]] [[H1004|that is in the house]] [[H3068|of the LORD.]] [[H589|“I]] [[H7592|am going to ask]] [[H1697|you something,”]] [[H559|said]] [[H4428|the king]] [[H413|to]] [[H3414|Jeremiah.]] [[H408|“Do not]] [[H3582|hide]] [[H1697|anything]] [[H4480|from me.”]] ^3814

[[H4428|But King]] [[H6667|Zedekiah]] [[H559|said]] [[H413|to]] [[H3414|Jeremiah,]] [[H589|“I]] [[H1672|am afraid]] [[H3064|of the Jews]] [[H834|who]] [[H5307|have deserted]] [[H413|to]] [[H3778|the Chaldeans,]] [[H6435|for]] ⟨the Chaldeans⟩ [[H5414|may hand me over to]] [[H3027|them]] [[H5953|to abuse me.”]] ^3819

[[H8672|And on the ninth]] [[H2320|day]] [[H7243|of the fourth]] [[H2320|month]] [[H6667|of Zedekiah’s]] [[H6249|eleventh]] [[H8141|year,]] [[H5892|the city]] [[H1234|was broken through.]] ^3902

[[H3605|Then all]] [[H8269|the officials]] [[H4428|of the king]] [[H894|of Babylon]] [[H935|entered]] [[H3427|and sat]] [[H8432|in the Middle]] [[H8179|Gate:]] [[H5371|Nergal-sharezer,]] [[H5562|Samgar,]] [[H8310|Nebusarsechim]] [[H7249|the Rab-saris,]] [[H5371|Nergal-sharezer]] [[H7248|the Rab-mag,]] [[H3605|and all]] [[H7611|the rest]] [[H8269|of the officials]] [[H4428|of the king]] [[H894|of Babylon.]] ^3903

[[H2428|But the army]] [[H3778|of the Chaldeans]] [[H7291|pursued]] [[H310|them]] [[H5381|and overtook]] [[H6667|Zedekiah]] [[H6160|in the plains]] [[H3405|of Jericho.]] [[H3947|They seized]] [[H853|him]] [[H5927|and brought him up]] [[H413|to]] [[H5019|Nebuchadnezzar]] [[H4428|king]] [[H894|of Babylon]] [[H7247|at Riblah]] [[H776|in the land]] [[H2574|of Hamath,]] [[H1696|where he pronounced]] [[H4941|judgment]] [[H853|on him.]] ^3905

[[H1697|This is the word]] [[H834|that]] [[H1961|came]] [[H413|to]] [[H3414|Jeremiah]] [[H4480|from]] [[H3068|the LORD]] [[H310|after]] [[H5018|Nebuzaradan]] [[H7227|the captain]] [[H2876|of the guard]] [[H7971|had released]] [[H853|him]] [[H7414|at Ramah,]] [[H3947|having found]] [[H1931|him]] [[H631|bound]] [[H246|in chains]] [[H8432|among]] [[H3605|all]] [[H1546|the captives]] [[H3389|of Jerusalem]] [[H3063|and Judah]] [[H1540|who were being exiled]] [[H894|to Babylon.]] ^4001

[[H3068|and now the LORD]] [[H935|has fulfilled it;]] [[H6213|He has done]] [[H834|just as]] [[H1696|He said.]] [[H3588|Because]] [[H2398|you have sinned]] ⟨people⟩ [[H3068|against the LORD]] [[H3808|and have not]] [[H8085|obeyed]] [[H6963|His voice,]] [[H2088|this]] [[H1697|thing]] [[H1961|has happened]] ^4003

[[H6258|But now,]] [[H2009|behold,]] [[H6605|I am freeing]] [[H3117|you today]] [[H4480|from]] [[H246|the chains]] [[H834|that]] [[H5921|were on]] [[H3027|your wrists.]] [[H518|If]] [[H2896|it pleases]] [[H935|you to come]] [[H854|with]] [[H894|me to Babylon,]] [[H935|then come,]] [[H7760|and I will take care of]] [[H5921|you.]] [[H518|But if]] [[H7489|it seems wrong]] [[H935|to you to come]] [[H854|with me]] [[H894|to Babylon,]] [[H2308|go no farther.]] [[H7200|Look,]] [[H3605|the whole]] [[H776|land]] [[H6440|is before you.]] [[H5869|Wherever it seems]] [[H2896|good]] [[H3477|and right]] [[H1980|for you to go,]] [[H1980|go]] [[H8033|there.]] ^4004

[[H3808|But before Jeremiah]] [[H7725|turned to go,]] [[H7725|Nebuzaradan]] [[H413|told him,]] [[H1436|“Return to Gedaliah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H296|of Ahikam,]] [[H1121|the son]] [[H8227|of Shaphan,]] [[H834|whom]] [[H4428|the king]] [[H894|of Babylon]] [[H6485|has appointed]] [[H5892|over the cities]] [[H3063|of Judah,]] [[H3427|and stay]] [[H854|with]] [[H8432|him among]] [[H5971|the people,]] [[H176|or]] [[H1980|go]] [[H413|anywhere else]] [[H3477|that seems right.]] [[H7227|Then the captain]] [[H2876|of the guard]] [[H5414|gave]] [[H737|him  a ration]] [[H4864|and a gift]] [[H7971|and released him.]] ^4005

[[H3414|So Jeremiah]] [[H935|went]] [[H413|to]] [[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H296|of Ahikam]] [[H4708|at Mizpah]] [[H3427|and stayed]] [[H854|with him]] [[H8432|among]] [[H5971|the people]] [[H7604|who were left]] [[H776|in the land.]] ^4006

[[H3605|When all]] [[H8269|the commanders]] [[H376|and men]] [[H2428|of the armies]] [[H7704|in the field]] [[H8085|heard]] [[H3588|that]] [[H4428|the king]] [[H894|of Babylon]] [[H6485|had appointed]] [[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H296|of Ahikam]] [[H776|over the land]] [[H3588|and that]] [[H6485|he had put him in charge]] [[H376|of the men,]] [[H802|women,]] [[H2945|and children]] ⟨who were⟩ [[H1803|the poorest]] [[H776|of the land]] ⟨and⟩ [[H834|]] [[H3808|had not]] [[H1540|been exiled]] [[H894|to Babylon,]] ^4007

[[H935|they came]] [[H413|to]] [[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H4708|at Mizpah—]] [[H3458|Ishmael]] [[H1121|son]] [[H5418|of Nethaniah,]] [[H3110|Johanan]] [[H3129|and Jonathan]] [[H1121|the sons]] [[H7143|of Kareah,]] [[H8304|Seraiah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H8576|of Tanhumeth,]] [[H1121|the sons]] [[H5778|of Ephai]] [[H5200|the Netophathite,]] [[H3153|and Jezaniah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H4602|of the Maacathite:]] [[H1992|they]] [[H582|and their men.]] ^4008

[[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H296|of Ahikam,]] [[H1121|the son]] [[H8227|of Shaphan,]] [[H7650|swore an oath]] [[H376|to them  and their men,]] [[H559|assuring them,]] [[H408|“Do not]] [[H3372|be afraid]] [[H5647|to serve]] [[H3778|the Chaldeans.]] [[H3427|Live]] [[H776|in the land]] [[H5647|and serve]] [[H4428|the king]] [[H894|of Babylon,]] [[H3190|and it will go well]] ^4009

[[H589|As for me,]] [[H2005|I will]] [[H3427|stay]] [[H4709|in Mizpah]] [[H5975|to represent]] [[H6440|you before]] [[H3778|the Chaldeans]] [[H834|who]] [[H935|come]] [[H413|to us.]] [[H859|As for you,]] [[H622|gather in]] [[H3196|wine,]] [[H7019|summer fruit,]] [[H8081|and oil,]] [[H7760|place them]] [[H3627|in your storage jars,]] [[H3427|and live]] [[H5892|in the cities]] [[H8610|you have taken over.]] ^4010

[[H3605|When all]] [[H3064|the Jews]] [[H4124|in Moab,]] [[H1121|Ammon,]] [[H123|Edom,]] [[H3605|and all]] [[H776|the other lands]] [[H8085|heard]] [[H3588|that]] [[H4428|the king]] [[H894|of Babylon]] [[H5414|had left]] [[H7611|a remnant]] [[H3063|in Judah]] [[H6485|and had appointed]] [[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H296|of Ahikam,]] [[H1121|the son]] [[H8227|of Shaphan,]] [[H5921|over them,]] ^4011

[[H3064|they]] [[H3605|all]] [[H7725|returned]] [[H3605|from all]] [[H4725|the places]] [[H834|to which]] [[H5080|they had been banished]] [[H935|and came]] [[H776|to the land]] [[H3063|of Judah,]] [[H413|to]] [[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H4708|at Mizpah.]] [[H622|And they gathered]] [[H7235|an abundance]] [[H3196|of wine]] [[H7019|and summer fruit.]] ^4012

[[H3110|Meanwhile, Johanan]] [[H1121|son]] [[H7143|of Kareah]] [[H3605|and all]] [[H8269|the commanders]] [[H2428|of the armies]] [[H7704|in the field]] [[H935|came]] [[H413|to]] [[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H4708|at Mizpah]] ^4013

[[H559|and said to him,]] [[H3045|“Are you aware]] [[H3588|that]] [[H1185|Baalis]] [[H4428|king]] [[H1121|of the Ammonites]] [[H7971|has sent]] [[H3458|Ishmael]] [[H1121|son]] [[H5418|of Nethaniah]] [[H5221|to take]] [[H5315|your life?”]] [[H1436|But Gedaliah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H296|of Ahikam]] [[H3808|did not]] [[H539|believe them.]] ^4014

[[H3110|Then Johanan]] [[H1121|son]] [[H7143|of Kareah]] [[H559|spoke]] [[H5643|privately]] [[H413|to]] [[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H4709|at Mizpah.]] [[H1980|“Let me go]] [[H5221|and kill]] [[H3458|Ishmael]] [[H1121|son]] [[H5418|of Nethaniah,”]] [[H559|he said.]] [[H3808|“No]] [[H376|one]] [[H3045|will know it.]] [[H4100|Why]] [[H5221|should he take]] [[H5315|your life]] [[H6327|and scatter]] [[H3605|all]] [[H3064|the Jews]] [[H6908|who have gathered]] [[H413|to you,]] [[H7611|so that the remnant]] [[H3063|of Judah]] [[H6|would perish?”]] ^4015

[[H1436|But Gedaliah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H296|of Ahikam]] [[H559|said]] [[H413|to]] [[H3110|Johanan]] [[H1121|son]] [[H7143|of Kareah,]] [[H408|“Do not]] [[H6213|do]] [[H1697|such a thing!]] [[H859|What you are]] [[H1696|saying]] [[H413|about]] [[H3458|Ishmael]] [[H8267|is a lie.”]] ^4016

[[H7637|In the seventh]] [[H2320|month,]] [[H3458|Ishmael]] [[H1121|son]] [[H5418|of Nethaniah,]] [[H1121|the son]] [[H476|of Elishama,]] ⟨who was a member⟩ [[H4410|of the royal]] [[H2233|family]] [[H4428|and one of the king’s]] [[H7227|chief officers,]] [[H935|came]] [[H854|with]] [[H6235|ten]] [[H376|men]] [[H413|to]] [[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H296|of Ahikam]] [[H4709|at Mizpah,]] [[H398|and they ate]] [[H3899|a meal]] [[H3162|together]] [[H8033|there.]] ^4101

[[H3458|Ishmael]] [[H1121|son]] [[H5418|of Nethaniah]] [[H6235|and the ten]] [[H376|men]] [[H834|who]] [[H1961|were]] [[H854|with]] [[H6965|him got up]] [[H5221|and struck down]] [[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H296|of Ahikam,]] [[H1121|the son]] [[H8227|of Shaphan,]] [[H2719|with the sword,]] [[H4191|killing]] [[H853|the one]] [[H834|whom]] [[H4428|the king]] [[H894|of Babylon]] [[H6485|had appointed to govern]] [[H776|the land.]] ^4102

[[H3458|Ishmael]] [[H5221|also killed]] [[H3605|all]] [[H3064|the Jews]] [[H834|who]] [[H1961|were]] [[H854|with]] [[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H4709|at Mizpah,]] [[H3778|as well as the Chaldean]] [[H4421|soldiers]] [[H834|who]] [[H8033|were there.]] ^4103

[[H8145|On the second]] [[H3117|day]] [[H4191|after the murder]] [[H1436|of Gedaliah,]] [[H3808|when no]] [[H376|one]] [[H3045|yet knew about it,]] ^4104

[[H8084|eighty]] [[H376|men]] [[H1548|who had shaved off]] [[H2206|their beards,]] [[H7167|torn]] [[H899|their garments,]] [[H1413|and cut themselves]] [[H935|came]] [[H7927|from Shechem,]] [[H7887|Shiloh,]] [[H8111|and Samaria,]] [[H3027|carrying]] [[H4503|grain offerings]] [[H3828|and incense]] [[H935|to bring]] [[H1004|to the temple]] [[H3068|of the LORD.]] ^4105

[[H3458|And Ishmael]] [[H1121|son]] [[H5418|of Nethaniah]] [[H3318|went out]] [[H4480|from]] [[H4709|Mizpah]] [[H7125|to meet them,]] [[H1058|weeping]] [[H1980|as he went.]] [[H6298|When encountered]] ⟨Ishmael⟩ ⟨the men⟩, [[H559|he said,]] [[H935|“Come]] [[H413|to]] [[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H296|of Ahikam.”]] ^4106

[[H935|And when they came]] [[H413|into]] [[H5892|the city,]] [[H3458|Ishmael]] [[H1121|son]] [[H5418|of Nethaniah]] [[H376|and the men]] [[H854|with him]] [[H7819|slaughtered them]] [[H413|and threw them into]] [[H953|a cistern.]] ^4107

[[H6235|But ten]] [[H376|of the men]] [[H4672|among them]] [[H559|said]] [[H413|to]] [[H3458|Ishmael,]] [[H408|“Do not]] [[H4191|kill us,]] [[H3588|for]] [[H3426|we have]] [[H4301|hidden treasure]] [[H7704|in the field—]] [[H2406|wheat,]] [[H8184|barley,]] [[H8081|oil,]] [[H1706|and honey!”]] [[H2308|So he refrained]] [[H4191|from killing them]] [[H8432|with]] [[H251|the others.]] ^4108

[[H953|Now the cistern]] [[H834|into which]] [[H3458|Ishmael]] [[H7993|had thrown]] [[H3605|all]] [[H6297|the bodies]] [[H376|of the men]] [[H5221|he had struck down]] [[H3027|along with]] [[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H834|was a large one that]] [[H4428|King]] [[H609|Asa]] [[H6213|had made]] [[H6440|for fear]] [[H1201|of Baasha]] [[H4428|king]] [[H3478|of Israel.]] [[H3458|Ishmael]] [[H1121|son]] [[H5418|of Nethaniah]] [[H4390|filled it]] [[H2491|with the slain.]] ^4109

[[H3458|Then Ishmael]] [[H7617|took captive]] [[H3605|all]] [[H7611|the remnant]] [[H5971|of the people]] [[H4709|of Mizpah—]] [[H1323|the daughters]] [[H4428|of the king]] [[H853|along with]] [[H3605|all]] [[H5971|the others]] [[H7604|who remained]] [[H4709|in Mizpah—]] [[H834|over whom]] [[H5018|Nebuzaradan]] [[H7227|the captain]] [[H2876|of the guard]] [[H6485|had appointed]] [[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H296|of Ahikam.]] [[H3458|Ishmael]] [[H1121|son]] [[H5418|of Nethaniah]] [[H7617|took them captive]] [[H1980|and set off]] [[H5674|to cross over]] [[H413|to]] [[H1121|the Ammonites.]] ^4110

[[H3110|When Johanan]] [[H1121|son]] [[H7143|of Kareah]] [[H3605|and all]] [[H8269|the commanders]] [[H2428|of the armies]] [[H854|with]] [[H853|him]] [[H8085|heard]] [[H3605|of all]] [[H7451|the crimes]] [[H834|that]] [[H3458|Ishmael]] [[H1121|son]] [[H5418|of Nethaniah]] [[H6213|had committed,]] ^4111

[[H3605|When all]] [[H5971|the people]] [[H854|with]] [[H3458|Ishmael]] [[H7200|saw]] [[H3110|Johanan]] [[H1121|son]] [[H7143|of Kareah]] [[H3605|and all]] [[H8269|the commanders]] [[H2428|of the army]] [[H854|with him,]] [[H8055|they rejoiced,]] ^4113

[[H3458|But Ishmael]] [[H1121|son]] [[H5418|of Nethaniah]] [[H8083|and eight]] ⟨of his⟩ [[H376|men]] [[H4422|escaped]] [[H6440|from]] [[H3110|Johanan]] [[H1980|and went]] [[H413|to]] [[H1121|the Ammonites.]] ^4115

[[H3110|Then Johanan]] [[H1121|son]] [[H7143|of Kareah]] [[H3605|and all]] [[H8269|the commanders]] [[H2428|of the armies]] [[H854|with him]] [[H3947|took]] [[H3605|the whole]] [[H7611|remnant]] [[H5971|of the people]] [[H4480|from]] [[H4709|Mizpah]] [[H834|whom]] [[H7725|he had recovered]] [[H3458|from Ishmael]] [[H1121|son]] [[H5418|of Nethaniah]] [[H310|after]] [[H5221|Ishmael had killed]] [[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H296|of Ahikam:]] [[H1397|the soldiers,]] [[H802|women,]] [[H2945|children,]] [[H5631|and court officials]] [[H7725|he had brought back]] [[H1391|from Gibeon.]] ^4116

[[H1980|And they went]] [[H3427|and stayed]] [[H1628|in Geruth]] [[H681|Chimham,]] [[H1035|near  Bethlehem,]] [[H1980|in order to proceed]] [[H4714|into Egypt]] ^4117

[[H6440|to escape]] [[H3778|the Chaldeans.]] [[H3588|For]] [[H3372|they were afraid]] [[H6440|of]] ⟨the Chaldeans⟩ [[H3588|because]] [[H3458|Ishmael]] [[H1121|son]] [[H5418|of Nethaniah]] [[H5221|had struck down]] [[H1436|Gedaliah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H296|of Ahikam,]] [[H834|whom]] [[H4428|the king]] [[H894|of Babylon]] [[H6485|had appointed]] [[H776|over the land.]] ^4118

[[H3605|Then all]] [[H8269|the commanders]] [[H2428|of the forces,]] [[H3110|along with Johanan]] [[H1121|son]] [[H7143|of Kareah,]] [[H3153|Jezaniah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H1955|of Hoshaiah,]] [[H3605|and all]] [[H5971|the people]] [[H6996|from the least]] [[H5704|to]] [[H1419|the greatest,]] [[H5066|approached]] ^4201

[[H3414|Jeremiah]] [[H5030|the prophet]] [[H559|and said,]] [[H8467|“May our petition]] [[H5307|come]] [[H6440|before you;]] [[H6419|pray]] [[H413|to]] [[H3068|the LORD]] [[H430|your God]] [[H1157|on behalf of]] [[H2063|this]] [[H3605|entire]] [[H7611|remnant.]] [[H3588|For]] [[H4592|few]] [[H7604|of us remain]] [[H7235|of the many,]] [[H834|as]] [[H7200|you can see]] [[H5869|with your own eyes.]] ^4202

⟨Pray⟩ [[H3069|that the LORD]] [[H430|your God]] [[H5046|may tell]] [[H1870|us the way]] [[H1980|we should walk]] [[H1697|and the thing]] [[H6213|we should do.”]] ^4203

[[H8085|“I have heard you,”]] [[H559|replied]] [[H3414|Jeremiah]] [[H5030|the prophet.]] [[H2005|“I will surely]] [[H6419|pray]] [[H413|to]] [[H3068|the LORD]] [[H430|your God]] [[H1697|as you request,]] [[H5046|and I will tell you]] [[H3605|everything]] [[H834|that]] [[H3068|the LORD]] [[H6030|answers;]] [[H3808|I will not]] [[H4513|withhold]] [[H1697|a word]] [[H4480|from you.”]] ^4204

[[H1992|Then they]] [[H559|said]] [[H413|to]] [[H3414|Jeremiah,]] [[H3068|“May the LORD]] [[H1961|be]] [[H571|a true]] [[H539|and faithful]] [[H5707|witness against us]] [[H518|if]] [[H3808|we do not]] [[H6213|act upon]] [[H3605|every]] [[H1697|word]] [[H834|that]] [[H3068|the LORD]] [[H430|your God]] [[H7971|sends you]] [[H413|to tell us.]] ^4205

[[H7093|After]] [[H6235|ten]] [[H3117|days,]] [[H1697|the word]] [[H3068|of the LORD]] [[H1961|came]] [[H413|to]] [[H3414|Jeremiah,]] ^4207

[[H7121|and he summoned]] [[H3110|Johanan]] [[H1121|son]] [[H7143|of Kareah,]] [[H3605|all]] [[H8269|the commanders]] [[H2428|of the forces]] [[H834|who]] [[H854|were with him,]] [[H3605|and all]] [[H5971|the people]] [[H6996|from the least]] [[H5704|to]] [[H1419|the greatest.]] ^4208

⟨Jeremiah⟩ [[H559|told]] [[H413|them,]] [[H3541|“Thus]] [[H559|says]] [[H3068|the LORD,]] [[H430|the God]] [[H3478|of Israel,]] [[H413|to]] [[H834|whom]] [[H7971|you sent]] [[H853|me]] [[H5307|to present]] [[H8467|your petition:]] ^4209

[[H518|If]] [[H3427|you will indeed stay]] [[H2063|in this]] [[H776|land,]] [[H1129|then I will build]] [[H853|you up]] [[H3808|and not]] [[H2040|tear you down;]] [[H5193|I will plant]] [[H853|you]] [[H3808|and not]] [[H5428|uproot you,]] [[H3588|for]] [[H5162|I shall relent]] [[H413|of]] [[H7451|the disaster]] [[H6213|I have brought]] ^4210

[[H408|Do not]] [[H3372|be afraid]] [[H4480|of]] [[H4428|the king]] [[H894|of Babylon,]] [[H834|whom]] [[H859|you]] [[H3373|now fear;]] [[H408|do not]] [[H3372|be afraid]] [[H6440|of him,]] [[H5002|declares]] [[H3068|the LORD,]] [[H3588|for]] [[H589|I]] [[H854|am with]] [[H3467|you to save]] [[H853|you]] [[H5337|and deliver]] [[H853|you]] [[H3027|from him.]] ^4211

[[H5414|And I will show]] [[H7356|you  compassion,]] [[H7355|and he will have compassion]] [[H853|on you]] [[H7725|and restore]] [[H853|you]] [[H413|to]] [[H127|your own land.]] ^4212

[[H518|But if]] [[H859|you]] [[H559|say,]] [[H3808|‘We will not]] [[H3427|stay]] [[H2063|in this]] [[H776|land,’]] [[H8085|and so disobey]] [[H6963|the voice]] [[H3068|of the LORD]] [[H430|your God,]] ^4213

[[H559|and if you say,]] [[H3808|‘No,]] [[H3588|but]] [[H935|we will go]] [[H776|to the land]] [[H4714|of Egypt]] [[H3427|and live]] [[H8033|there,]] [[H834|where]] [[H3808|we will not]] [[H7200|see]] [[H4421|war,]] [[H8085|or hear]] [[H6963|the sound]] [[H7782|of the trumpet,]] [[H7456|or hunger]] [[H3899|for food,’]] ^4214

[[H6258|then]] [[H8085|hear]] [[H1697|the word]] [[H3068|of the LORD,]] [[H7611|O remnant]] [[H3063|of Judah!]] [[H3541|This is what]] [[H3068|the LORD]] [[H6635|of Hosts,]] [[H430|the God]] [[H3478|of Israel,]] [[H559|says:]] [[H518|If]] [[H859|you]] [[H7760|are determined]] [[H935|to go]] [[H4714|to Egypt]] [[H1481|and reside]] [[H8033|there,]] ^4215

[[H2719|then the sword]] [[H859|you]] [[H3372|fear]] [[H5381|will overtake]] [[H853|you]] [[H8033|there,]] [[H7458|and the famine]] [[H859|you]] [[H1672|dread]] [[H1692|will follow on your heels]] [[H4714|into Egypt,]] [[H4191|and you will die]] [[H8033|there.]] ^4216

[[H3605|So all]] [[H834|who]] [[H7760|resolve]] [[H935|to go]] [[H4714|to Egypt]] [[H8033|to reside there]] [[H1961|will]] [[H4191|die]] [[H2719|by the sword,]] [[H7458|famine,]] [[H1698|and plague.]] [[H3808|Not one]] [[H1961|of them will]] [[H8300|survive]] [[H6412|or escape]] [[H7451|the disaster]] [[H589|I]] [[H935|will bring]] [[H5921|upon them.]] ^4217

[[H3588|For]] [[H3541|this is what]] [[H3068|the LORD]] [[H6635|of Hosts,]] [[H430|the God]] [[H3478|of Israel,]] [[H559|says:]] [[H834|‘Just as]] [[H639|My anger]] [[H2534|and wrath]] [[H5413|were poured out]] [[H5921|on]] [[H3427|the residents]] [[H3389|of Jerusalem,]] [[H3651|so]] [[H2534|will My wrath]] [[H5413|be poured out]] [[H5921|on you]] [[H935|if you go]] [[H4714|to Egypt.]] [[H1961|You will become]] [[H423|an object of cursing]] [[H8047|and horror,]] [[H7045|of vilification]] [[H2781|and disgrace,]] [[H3808|and you will never]] [[H7200|see]] [[H2088|this]] [[H4725|place]] [[H5750|again.]] ^4218

[[H3068|The LORD]] [[H1696|has told]] [[H5921|you,]] [[H7611|O remnant]] [[H3063|of Judah,]] [[H408|‘Do not]] [[H935|go]] [[H4714|to Egypt.’]] [[H3045|Know]] [[H3045|for sure]] [[H3588|that]] [[H5749|I have warned]] [[H3117|you  today!]] ^4219

[[H3588|For]] [[H5315|you]] [[H8582|have deceived]] [[H859|yourselves]] [[H7971|by sending]] [[H853|me]] [[H413|to]] [[H3068|the LORD]] [[H430|your God,]] [[H559|saying,]] [[H6419|‘Pray]] [[H413|to]] [[H3068|the LORD]] [[H430|our God]] [[H5704|on our behalf,]] [[H3605|and as for all]] [[H834|that]] [[H3068|the LORD]] [[H430|our God]] [[H559|says,]] [[H5046|tell it to us,]] [[H6213|and we will do it.]] ^4220

[[H6258|Now therefore,]] [[H3045|know]] [[H3045|for sure]] [[H3588|that]] [[H2719|by the sword,]] [[H7458|famine,]] [[H1698|and plague]] [[H4191|you will die]] [[H4725|in the place]] [[H834|where]] [[H2654|you desire]] [[H935|to go]] [[H1481|to reside.”]] ^4222

[[H3414|When Jeremiah]] [[H3615|had finished]] [[H1696|telling]] [[H3605|all]] [[H5971|the people]] [[H3605|all]] [[H1697|the words]] [[H3068|of the LORD]] [[H430|their God—]] [[H3605|everything that]] [[H3068|the LORD]] [[H7971|had sent him]] [[H413|to —]] ⟨say⟩ ^4301

[[H5838|then Azariah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H1955|of Hoshaiah,]] [[H3110|Johanan]] [[H1121|son]] [[H7143|of Kareah,]] [[H3605|and all]] [[H2086|the arrogant]] [[H376|men]] [[H559|said]] [[H413|to]] [[H3414|Jeremiah,]] [[H859|“You]] [[H8267|are lying!]] [[H3068|The LORD]] [[H430|our God]] [[H3808|has not]] [[H7971|sent]] [[H559|you to say,]] [[H3808|‘You must not]] [[H935|go]] [[H4714|to Egypt]] [[H8033|to reside there.]] ^4302
